【UNABLE TO CREATE REFER NOTE ON STO RECEIVING】
问题: UNABLE TO CREATE REFER NOTE ON STO RECEIVING

根因分类: SAP Std Functionality

具体根因: Software - SAP Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:

unable to create refere note due to 1 DN number has an error message
line delivery no.20
DN#0074834849[20589394]MS-MUSTARD FLAV_SALMON CHIPS-360G
Packaging unit master data do

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause: 
There is one article (20589394) included in the BST without barcode upon creation of STO the reason why the store cannot receive the reference SEAL.

Solution:
Coordinated to DC to process the reversal of the affected Delivery 74834849.
Upon reversal, Advise the store to Pull again the original seal to download those valid deliveries for receive
DC split the reversed delivery since there's other valid article included in the DN to be able separate from invalid article.
After splitting (another new delivery number is created) DC post GI this DN with valid article using a new seal (1317313) and delete the original DN with invalid article, for creation of new STO.
Re-create the new DN-74922913 with corrected article and new seal.(1317344)
Advise the Store to receive also the two newly created seal to receive the affected articles.

【POS DEVICE HAS NOT BEEN CONFIGURED】
问题: POS DEVICE HAS NOT BEEN CONFIGURED

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Configuration / Setup Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

POS 7 UNABLE TO USE.RESPOSE: "The device has not been configured."

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:POS device is unable to proceed to the Login page and remains stuck on the application boot screen.
Error: The device has not been configured. Start to register? (UAT environment)

Root Cause Analysis:The issue was caused by incorrect environment configuration in the POS release package.
After the POS was manually forced to restart, the environment parameter was incorrectly set to UAT instead of PROD.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.R&D confirmed that due to the incorrect environment setting, the POS application failed to complete the initialization process. 
As a result, the Login module could not be loaded, and the POS screen displayed the error message: “The device has not been configured. Start to register?”
3. Asked approval from Maam Chanda to correct the environment parameter in the App.json and version.dat files from "UAT" to "PRO" as a temporary solution.
4. Informed Maam Chanda and the store that the POS is now operational and can be used normally.
5.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

Image 1. POS application boot screen error



Image 2. App.json file environment parameter




Image 3. version.dat file environment parameter

As we checked with our R&D team, we found that all transaction data of POS 007 is stored in the ISP database. Please see the image below for reference.


To transfer all transactions of POS 007 to the cloud, we need to export the data from the ISP and import it into the cloud. After the data is imported into the cloud, we will manually regenerate the EOD file.


The sales for January 14, 2026 is already imported to the Cloud from ISP. (Sales already exist).


Resolved.​

Response Level:Level A

already successful to pull the BST Seal # 1316878-80 in D-mall web, but in PDA once input to create refer Note the seal # 1316878-80 pop-up " document is not availa

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:

Seal number: 13

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:

【Unable to Process STO Seal#】
问题: Unable to Process STO Seal#

根因分类: Wrong Master Data (SAP)

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:

Issue: Unable to process / receive DC to store Seal #

SEAL # 1316452-54
Plate #: NIC 5989G.I 641 of DC: January 13, 2026

Status:
- Actual item already received
- Seal # / ST

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause: 
There is one article (20589394) included in the BST without barcode upon creation of STO the reason why the store cannot receive the reference SEAL.

Solution:
Coordinated to DC to process the reversal of the affected Delivery 74834850.
Upon reversal, Advise the store to Pull again the original seal to download those valid deliveries for receive
DC split the reversed delivery since there's other valid article included in the DN to be able separate from invalid article.
After splitting (another new delivery number is created) DC post GI this DN with valid article using a new seal (1317320) and delete the original DN with invalid article, for creation of new STO.
Re-create the new DN-74838057 with corrected article and new seal.(1317339)
Advise the Store to receive also the two newly created seal to receive the affected articles.

【SLOC - 0003 WITH NEGATIVE SYSTEM INVTY】
问题: SLOC - 0003 WITH NEGATIVE SYSTEM INVTY

根因分类: Service Request

具体根因: Software - Client Request

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:level B
Details of Issue:

KIndly check why SLOC -0003 (BO LOCATION) has negative inventories despite with NOT ALLOW in the configuration settings as per management requirement.. See below SS;

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define
Issue:SLOC - 0003 WITH NEGATIVE SYSTEM INVTYRoot
Cause Analysis:Service Request
Resolution:
Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated checked the issue in DMall.
We conducted an inventory comparison and identified that the negative balance in SLoc 003 was caused by a failed TP (due to a locking issue) during the creation of an RPO. Instead of reposting the failed TP, it was reversed. As a result, the RPO claimed the allocated inventory for another RPO.
In this scenario, RPO A creation(TP inventory from 001 to 003) was reversed due to locking then the RPO A was claimed but no more allocated inventory for it thus occupying inventory for RPO B. After it was claimed, the TP for RPO B was rejected and since there is no more inventory for it and the system's design doesn't check the inventory, it resulted to a negative inventory.
After communicating this to Sir Elvis, he advised that since there is no inventory in SLoc 003, the inventory movement should failed since SLoc 003 should not allow negative inventory.
We coordinated this to our R&D, and it was confirmed, that this should be added to our problem management as problem #337.
Proceeds in resolving the ticket.
Release
Notes/Version: -
Remarks/Recommendation:
-
Data
Collection/References:

FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Issue: PO change in vendor
Solution:
The transaction was successfully posted in DMall; however, it did not integrate into SAP. To reverse the inventory that was added due to the Goods Receipt (GR) of this PO:
a. The store will submit a request letter to OPC as documentation for the reversal of the inventory in the DMall system.
b. Once the request is received, OPC will execute the “UNDO” function for the specific PO. This action reverses the inventory in SAP.
c. DMall will then tag the reference order as “NO NEED.”

【SMCo Tanay [0792] IBMS Integration logs 2026 JANUARY 17 - Error Msg: Deficit of SL Unrestricted-use 14 PC : 20349051 0792 0003】
问题: SMCo Tanay [0792] IBMS Integration logs 2026 JANUARY 17 - Error Msg: Deficit of SL Unrestricted-use 14 PC : 20349051 0792 0003

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: New Ticket Creation Template






Contact Person: *




DMall Support Team






Contact Number / MS Teams: *




09686165958






Email Address: *




dmall2helpdesk@dmall.com






AD ID: *




FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:
The issue was caused by a double settlement made by the store and OPC Lizha. The store had already executed the TP-Back from SLOC 0003 to SLOC 0001 for the partial RTV. However, the proposed solution involved clicking the “Transfer Post” button in Order Query, which was executed by OPC Lizha after the RPO settlement was completed by the store. This resulted in an inventory deficit.

Resolution:
The store submitted the required documents, and OPC performed movement 170 in SLOC 1 and 171 in SLOC 3 for 14 pieces of the affected article 20349051. Dmall will tag order number IO10792202601170005 as “No Need” once approved by the IT heads.

【No generated EOD】
问题: No generated EOD

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Configuration / Setup Issue

问题描述: Type:No generated EOD
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:
No generated EOD for Jan. 18, 2025

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:FOR CONFIGURATION OF POS

Root Cause Analysis: Defect from Dmall

Resolution:
Issue Summary
The affected POS device is unable to proceed to the Login page and remains stuck on the application boot screen as shown in the screenshot below.

Image 1. POS application boot screen error

Root Cause
The issue was caused by incorrect environment configuration in the POS release package.
After the POS was manually forced to restart, the environment parameter was incorrectly set to UAT instead of PROD.

Impact
Due to the incorrect environment setting, the POS application failed to complete the initialization process.
As a result, the Login module could not be loaded, and the POS screen displayed the error message:
“The device has not been configured. Start to register?”

Resolution / Next Steps
Temporary Solution: The environment configuration of the affected POS needs to be corrected back to PROD to allow proper initialization and normal access to the Login page.
Change the "env" parameter in the App.json file from "UAT" to "PRO" and save it.

Image 2. App.json file environment parameter

Change the "RELEASE_ENV" parameter in the version.dat file from "UAT" to "PRO" and save it.


Image 3. version.dat file environment parameter

Open and run the DMall POS application.

Long-term Solution:
This has been added to Problem 302.
Need to repackage the release file with PROD environment setting.
Has been deployed in the UAT environment for testing of SM IT under 202601_4_PRODFIX_POS release.

Advise the store that they can now use the POS.

Ticket resolved.

【unsuccessful gr posting of sto # 2035244489 received as not served and still hanging in SAP intransit】
问题: unsuccessful gr posting of sto # 2035244489 received as not served and still hanging in SAP intransit

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:
Goods receieving still at "POSTING" status in SAP POST after process stdr receiving "NOT SERVED" FOR REFERENCE sto#2035244489for article20213228

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Issue:The system does not support the "Not Served" status when the store does not receive all items listed under the Document Number (DN) or Seal Number. This scenario had not been encountered previously, as there was no prior instance where the issuing site failed to deliver all items to the store. 
This issue has also been documented in our Problem Management system under Problem 183.

Resolution: Dmall to proceed with generating the STDR

【SSM CEBU [0319] MySQL Timeout Exception Error】
问题: SSM CEBU [0319] MySQL Timeout Exception Error

根因分类: Defect from SM

具体根因: Apps - Deadlock or SQL Timeout

问题描述: Good day!







This ticket is filed for documentation purposes regarding the MySQL service issue encountered on the
SSM Cebu ISPon January 8, 2026, as shown in the screenshot below.


The issue observed was that the ISP MySQL servi

解决摘要: Application Reinstallation

解决方案:
Define Issue:SSM CEBU [0319] MySQL Timeout Exception Error

Root Cause Analysis:ISP MySQL service repeatedly terminated unexpectedly
Based on theSQL error logs, issue may be caused by a MySQL bug, database corruption, or an abnormal interruption that resulted in storage engine file corruption.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.The MySQL84 service and the ISP application were restarted. Although the services were able to start, the MySQL service continued to time out automatically.
3.Based on the CPU Resource Monitoring information, themysqld.exeprocess was being automatically terminated, resulting in the failure to establish a JDBC connection.
4. Checked the SQL error logs. According to our R&D team, the issue may be caused by a MySQL bug, database corruption, or an abnormal interruption that resulted in storage engine file corruption.
5. Advised SM IT to backup the ISP data and application folders, then reinstall/reimage the ISP of SSM Cebu. Provided them the Procedure document for the required backup steps/guidelines prior to reinstallation or reimaging.
6. SM IT deactivated the old ISP then activated the new created ISP VM.
7. SM IT confirmed thatthe new ISP of SSM Cebu is already up and running.
8.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References: 

Image 1. SSM Cebu's ISP MySQL service alert


Image 2. MySQL84 service status


Image 3. CPU Resource Monitoring information


Image 4.SQL error logs

【APPROVAL MATRIX CONCERN ON DISPOSAL & SCRAPPING】
问题: APPROVAL MATRIX CONCERN ON DISPOSAL & SCRAPPING

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Program Bug

问题描述: Type: Incident / RequestAPPROVAL MATRIX CONCERN ON DISPOSAL & SCRAPPINGResponse Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

Per Matrix the Approval Matrix for Disposal & Scrapping to reach President's Approval is P50,000.01 and A

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:APPROVAL MATRIX CONCERN ON DISPOSAL & SCRAPPING

Root Cause Analysis: Defect from Dmall

Resolution:

Upon verification by our R&D team, they have confirmed that this is a system bug. The current configuration routes transactions with values between these amounts incorrectly, due to improper handling of decimal values.
Proposed Short-Term Solutions (Options):Option 1:Proceed with the approval
Option 2:Rollback the created transactions

Long-Term Solution:
Add the issue to the problem list no. 311 for a permanent fix.

Remarks/Recommendation:

【POS UAT/TESTING ENVIRONMENT】
问题: POS UAT/TESTING ENVIRONMENT

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Configuration / Setup Issue

问题描述: Type:POS UAT/TESTING ENVIRONMENT
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:

FOR YOUR ASSISTANCE POS 21 , POS 39 , AND POS 21 ARE IN UAT/TESTING ENVIRONMENT.


THANKS!

解决摘要: Temporary / Quick Solution (Workaround)

解决方案:
Define Issue:POS device is unable to proceed to the Login page and remains stuck on the application boot screen.
Error: The device has not been configured. Start to register? (UAT environment)

Root Cause Analysis:The issue was caused by incorrect environment configuration in the POS release package.
After the POS was manually forced to restart, the environment parameter was incorrectly set to UAT instead of PROD.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.R&D confirmed that due to the incorrect environment setting, the POS application failed to complete the initialization process. 
As a result, the Login module could not be loaded, and the POS screen displayed the error message: “The device has not been configured. Start to register?”
3. Asked approval from Maam Chanda to correct the environment parameter in the App.json and version.dat files from "UAT" to "PRO" as a temporary solution.
4. Informed Maam Chanda and the store that the POS is now operational and can be used normally.
5.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-

【sloc 0003 articles with negative inventories】
问题: sloc 0003 articles with negative inventories

根因分类: Service Request

具体根因: Software - Client Request

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:

Articles at SLOC 0003 with negative inventories which are for OPC's settlement. Upon verification negative inventories are BUG inventories.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:sloc 0003 articles with negative inventories​Root Cause Analysis:Service Request

Resolution:
Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated checked the issue in DMall.
We conducted an inventory comparison and identified that the negative balance in SLoc 003 was caused by a failed TP (due to a locking issue) during the creation of an RPO. Instead of reposting the failed TP, it was reversed. As a result, the RPO claimed the allocated inventory for another RPO.
In this scenario, RPO A creation(TP inventory from 001 to 003) was reversed due to locking then the RPO A was claimed but no more allocated inventory for it thus occupying inventory for RPO B. After it was claimed, the TP for RPO B was rejected and since there is no more inventory for it and the system's design doesn't check the inventory, it resulted to a negative inventory.
After communicating this to Sir Elvis, he advised that since there is no inventory in SLoc 003, the inventory movement should failed since SLoc 003 should not allow negative inventory.
We coordinated this to our R&D, and it was confirmed, that this should be added to our problem management as problem #337.
Proceeds in resolving the ticket.
Release Notes/Version: -
Remarks/Recommendation: -
Data Collection/References:

【NO EOD FILES】

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

SSM LAS PINAS CITY "LP" (0727)
-Upon checking with successful EOD but NO EOD files created.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:No generated EOD files for SVI SJDM TD: 10/11/2025

Root Cause Analysis:- On POS036, during the transaction of SI#559201036260124165007060123, the customer paid thru gcash and already deducted on his/her account, but due to the"poor connection"of the POS, it exceeds the waiting time and the message pops up"Cancel, Retry and Mark Success".
- Cashier clicks the "Mark Success". Since this function needs an authorization, she got confused and decided to exit the application and restart the POS(hardware) , and when the POS opens up, she chose BDO Credit instead since the customer already deducted on his/her gcash account.

2. Asked approval to fix the affected transaction.
3. R&D markedthe "GCash INT" payment status to "Payment Failed" in the Cloud database and reran the EOD files.

【UNABLE TO USE POS 33 OF DMALL POS DUE TO REQUIRED FOR DEVISE INITIALIZATION】
问题: UNABLE TO USE POS 33 OF DMALL POS DUE TO REQUIRED FOR DEVISE INITIALIZATION

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Configuration / Setup Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request UNABLE TO USE POS 33/ NEED DEVISE INITIALIZATION
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue: SINCE WE HAVE SCHEDULE POWER SHUTDOWN LAST NIGHT AND ALL POS WERE SHUT DOWN, UPON CHECKING TODAY POS 33 IS REQUIREING

解决摘要: Temporary / Quick Solution (Workaround)

解决方案:
Define Issue:POS device is unable to proceed to the Login page and remains stuck on the application boot screen.
Error: The device has not been configured. Start to register? (UAT environment)

Root Cause Analysis:The issue was caused by incorrect environment configuration in the POS release package.
After the POS was manually forced to restart, the environment parameter was incorrectly set to UAT instead of PROD.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.R&D confirmed that due to the incorrect environment setting, the POS application failed to complete the initialization process. 
As a result, the Login module could not be loaded, and the POS screen displayed the error message: “The device has not been configured. Start to register?”
3. Asked approval from Maam Chanda to correct the environment parameter in the App.json and version.dat files from "UAT" to "PRO" as a temporary solution.
4. Informed Maam Chanda and the store that the POS is now operational and can be used normally.
5.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

Image 1. POS application boot screen error



Image 2. App.json file environment parameter




Image 3. version.dat file environment parameter

1. Store must submit all required documents for settlement directly to OPC (do not attach signed-off documents in Manage Engine due to DPA concerns). Submissions should include a detailed list of articles with quantities, reference STO document, and posting date.
2. Since there is no reversal of 937 in DMall, OPC will do the reversal in SAP (movement 938) which will revert the inventory in sloc 0007 of store.
3. OPC will perform TP 311 from Sloc 0007 to Sloc 0001 of store in SAP.
4. OPC will manually adjust the inventory in Sloc 0001 of store using movement 171 (increased) in DMall.

【STO POST FAILED STATUS AT DMALL OS ALREADY HAVE DN #】
问题: STO POST FAILED STATUS AT DMALL OS ALREADY HAVE DN #

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Type: Request
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue: Failed posting to GR. Upon checking already have DN # but still POST FAILED in DMALL OS. Already try to RE-POST but still on Post Failed status
STO #: 2035872980
DN # : 0074969057
POS

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root cause:
Based on our review, the error was caused by aduplicate line item.In the DMall system,Delivery Note (DN) creation and Goods Issuance (GI)are executed as a single, simultaneous process, whereas in SAP these are handled astwo separate steps. At the time the DN and GI were created in DMall, article20571937had an available inventory of9 PC. However, DMall allowed the issuance oftwo sets of 9 PCfor the same article, which resulted innegative inventory.In SAP, theGoods Issuance (movement type 921)was not successful because onlyone DNfor article20571937with a quantity of9 PCcould be issued, as this was the total available inventory.

Solution:
OPCissuedDN 0074969057and completed the receipt viaMIGOin SAP.
OPCperformedGR 171inSLoc 0001of the receiving store (1085 SMCO Marulas) in DMall, ensuring that the adjustments are aligned with the postedGR 101in SAP.
OPCperformedGR 171for article20571937inSLoc 0001of the issuing site (2064 SMCO One Mall) to offset the negative inventory in DMall

Define Issue:SMCo KINGHOME TANZA [5995] Integration Inventory 2026 January 26 - Material 10189227 5995 0003 does not exist Deficit of SL Unrestricted-use 5 PC : 20334211 5995 0003
Root Cause Analysis: Timing issue

Resolution:
Created a Integration Ticket.
Coordinated to Functional.
As per Functional, the error occurred due to an incorrect sequence of data sent to SAP. RO261Q202 was created and rejected within one minute (January 26, 2025 at 16:24 and 16:25). The transfer posting from SLOC 0003 to SLOC 0001 was sent to SAP first, ahead of the transfer posting from SLOC 0001 to SLOC 0003, which resulted in a deficit for the affected articles.



However, the transaction was pushed through in Dmall but was not posted in SAP.

To resolve this issue, Dmall will manually repost Order No. IO15995202601260005.

解决方案:
Define Issue:POS pre-commit data is not accurate

Root Cause Analysis:POS connection issue / Offline ISP
POS can't connect to the ISP and Cloud during shift handover; uses the POS local data.

Resolution:

【UNTALLY INVENTORY】
问题: UNTALLY INVENTORY

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Resolved Without Action / Support

问题描述: Type:UNTALLY INVENTORY
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue: I DON'T KNOW HOW TO REMOVE THE TOGUE AND TURNIP FROM MY NEGATIVE INVENTORY, I DON'T KNOW IF I MADE A MISTAKE IN THE PROCESS OF 1111 & 981

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause Analysis:I DON'T KNOW HOW TO REMOVE THE TOGUE AND TURNIP FROM MY NEGATIVE INVENTORY, I DON'T KNOW IF I MADE A MISTAKE IN THE PROCESS OF 1111 & 981

Resolution: Upon checking, articles 20302520 and 20302519 are ModCon articles without inventory, which means there is no inventory for these items. In SAP, there is a job that automatically reverses the sales for ModCon articles without inventory, bringing the inventory back to zero. Similarly, in DMall, movement type 176 zeroes out the inventory for ModCon articles without inventory; this job was deployed last February 4.​

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

SMCO La Trinidad (1228)-Perform manual reconciliation but still no EOD files generated

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:No generated EOD files for SMCo La Trinidad TD: 1/29/2026

Root Cause Analysis:
Store 1228 Cutover date was on 1/28/2026 and Go-live was on 1/29/2026.
A positive sales transaction(Receipt No. 560056002260129020052170001)was processed on January 29, 2026 at 2:02 AM and was subsequently voided at 2:39 AM on the same day.
This transaction includesArticle 20494684, which was delisted in SAP on January 28, 2026 and integrated into DMall on January 29, 2026 at 2:07 AM.
Since Article 20494684 no longer exists in Store 1228, the EOD file generation verification logic is unable to locate the article during validation.
As a result, the system fails to generate the EOD files.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed SM team about the findings, root cause and the temporary solution. Added toProblem No. 321.
3. Askedfor SM assistance and approval to proceed with the necessary corrective actions.
4. Informed them thatDMall recommends to temporarily list/restore the article 20494684 in SMCo La Trinidadand wait for the EOD files to generate automatically before delisting it again.
5. Masterdata confirmed that the article was already relisted. Informed them that the EOD files were already generated.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:
Image 1. Receipt No 560056002260129020052170001 Order Details



Image 2. After-Sales Receipt No9560056002260129023938011 Order Details




Image 3.Article 20494684 delisted sync time








Image 4. Generated EOD files

AD ID: *




FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:
The error occurred because the user selected the wrong movement type (911). Based on our checking the said articles that user intend to process were Non Trade with valuation class 3103 and 3104 which are not supposed to be process in movement 911 - GR Excess Premium

Solution:
1. Advise the store to submit request letter for settlement to OPC.
2. OPC performs an "undo" operation to automatically reverse the transaction and updates the undo status to "yes."
3. DMall tagged the SAP Post status of the transaction to "No Need".

【cannot process seal #0281104-06】
问题: cannot process seal #0281104-06

根因分类: Support Group Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

Good day
We would like to seek for assistance regarding in. please see attached file.
seal #:0281104-06
ERP#2035626083 AND2035567846

thank you

ryan

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:
Based on our review,Seal 0281104-06was already used to receiveDN 0074797879on12/21/2025.Subsequently,STO 2035626083withDN 0074777961andSTO 2035567846withDN 0074744004were assigned toSeal 0281104-06on12/23/2025and were downloaded in DMall the following day. As a result, the store was unable to processSeal 0281104-06.

Solution:
DC updated the sealforDN 0074777961andDN 0074744004, then advised the store to receive the deliveries using thenew seal.
